			value = 940
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			gdp_var > 945000000
			or = {
				capital_gdp_ratio < 0.5
				root.num_states <3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = gdp_view_fc
			value = 945
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			gdp_var > 950000000
			or = {
				capital_gdp_ratio < 0.5
				root.num_states <3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = gdp_view_fc
			value = 950
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			gdp_var > 955000000
			or = {
				capital_gdp_ratio < 0.5
				root.num_states <3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = gdp_view_fc
			value = 955
		}
	}
	if = {

				root.num_states <3

		set_variable = {

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			gdp_var > 965000000
			or = {
				capital_gdp_ratio < 0.5
				root.num_states <3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = gdp_view_fc
			value = 965
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			gdp_var > 970000000
			or = {
				capital_gdp_ratio < 0.5
				root.num_states <3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = gdp_view_fc
			value = 970
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			gdp_var > 975000000

				capital_gdp_ratio < 0.5
				root.num_states <3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = gdp_view_fc
			value = 975

	}
	if = {

	if = {

	if = {

				root.num_states <3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = gdp_view_fc
			value = 1000
		}
	}

central_bank_modifier = {
	capital = {
		save_scope_as = capital_scope
	}
	every_scope_state = { #historic_place jamais netoyer
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = central_bank_place
			}
			remove_modifier = central_bank_place
		}
	}
	scope:capital_scope = { #actualisation capital
		#place
		if = {
			limit = {
				not = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_place
				}
			}
			remove_modifier = central_bank_place
			add_modifier = {
				name = central_bank_place
			}
		}
		#historic_place
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = central_bank_place
			}
			remove_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
			add_modifier = {
				name = central_bank_historic_place
			}
		}
	}
	if = { #country - une seul fois
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = {
				has_building = building_bank
			}
			not  = {
				has_modifier = has_central_bank
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = has_central_bank
		}
	}
	if = { #country_already_central_bank
		limit = {
			# any_scope_state = {
			# 	has_building = building_bank
			# }
			has_building = building_bank
			not = {
				var:country_already_central_bank = 1
			}
		}
		set_variable  = {
			name = country_already_central_bank
			value = 1
		}
	}
}
financial_center_modifier = {
    every_scope_state = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_modifier = financial_center_place
            }
            remove_modifier = financial_center_place
        }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = financial_center_place_spe
			}
			remove_modifier = financial_center_place_spe
		}
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_modifier = financial_center_historic_place
            }
            remove_modifier = financial_center_historic_place
        }
		set_variable = {
			name = financial_center_site_var
			value = 0
		}
    }

	#reg
	capital = {
        if = {
            limit = {
				building_financial_centre_spe = no
				has_building = building_financial_centre
            }
			if = {
				limit = {
					not = {
						has_modifier = financial_center_place
					}
				}
				remove_modifier = financial_center_place
				add_modifier = {
					name = financial_center_place
					multiplier = var:gdp_view_fc
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					and = {
						has_modifier = financial_center_place
						not = {
							has_modifier = financial_center_historic_place
						}
					}
				}
				remove_modifier = financial_center_historic_place
				add_modifier = {
					name = financial_center_historic_place
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = financial_center_site_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
    }
	#spe
	every_scope_state = {
        if = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					has_building = building_financial_centre_arg
					has_building = building_financial_centre_aus
					has_building = building_financial_centre_bav
					has_building = building_financial_centre_bel
					has_building = building_financial_centre_bic
					has_building = building_financial_centre_brz
					has_building = building_financial_centre_chi
					has_building = building_financial_centre_chl
					has_building = building_financial_centre_den
					has_building = building_financial_centre_dei
					has_building = building_financial_centre_egy
					has_building = building_financial_centre_fra
					has_building = building_financial_centre_frm
					has_building = building_financial_centre_gbr
					has_building = building_financial_centre_gbr_2
					has_building = building_financial_centre_gre
					has_building = building_financial_centre_hkh
					has_building = building_financial_centre_han
					has_building = building_financial_centre_ita
					has_building = building_financial_centre_jap
					has_building = building_financial_centre_mex
					has_building = building_financial_centre_net
					has_building = building_financial_centre_nsw
					has_building = building_financial_centre_ont
					has_building = building_financial_centre_peu
					has_building = building_financial_centre_por
					has_building = building_financial_centre_pru
					has_building = building_financial_centre_que
					has_building = building_financial_centre_rus
					has_building = building_financial_centre_saf
					has_building = building_financial_centre_sar
					has_building = building_financial_centre_sic
					has_building = building_financial_centre_spa
					has_building = building_financial_centre_swe
					has_building = building_financial_centre_swi
					has_building = building_financial_centre_tus
					has_building = building_financial_centre_tur
					has_building = building_financial_centre_uru
					has_building = building_financial_centre_usa
					has_building = building_financial_centre_usa_2
					has_building = building_financial_centre_sax
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = financial_center_place_spe
				}
				remove_modifier = financial_center_place_spe
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = financial_center_place_spe
				multiplier = var:gdp_view_fc
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					and = {
						has_modifier = financial_center_place_spe
						not = {
							has_modifier = financial_center_historic_place
						}
					}
				}
				remove_modifier = financial_center_historic_place
				add_modifier = {
					name = financial_center_historic_place
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = financial_center_site_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
    }

	#####################################################################################################################################################
	# boucle pour les modificateur

	if = { #country
		limit = {
			or = {
				has_building = building_financial_centre
				has_building = building_financial_centre_arg
				has_building = building_financial_centre_aus
				has_building = building_financial_centre_bav
				has_building = building_financial_centre_bel
				has_building = building_financial_centre_bic
				has_building = building_financial_centre_brz
				has_building = building_financial_centre_chi
				has_building = building_financial_centre_chl
				has_building = building_financial_centre_den
				has_building = building_financial_centre_dei
				has_building = building_financial_centre_egy
				has_building = building_financial_centre_fra
				has_building = building_financial_centre_frm
				has_building = building_financial_centre_gbr
				has_building = building_financial_centre_gbr_2
				has_building = building_financial_centre_gre
				has_building = building_financial_centre_hkh
				has_building = building_financial_centre_han
				has_building = building_financial_centre_ita
				has_building = building_financial_centre_jap
				has_building = building_financial_centre_mex
				has_building = building_financial_centre_net
				has_building = building_financial_centre_nsw
				has_building = building_financial_centre_ont
				has_building = building_financial_centre_peu
				has_building = building_financial_centre_por
				has_building = building_financial_centre_pru
				has_building = building_financial_centre_que
				has_building = building_financial_centre_rus
				has_building = building_financial_centre_saf
				has_building = building_financial_centre_sar
				has_building = building_financial_centre_sic
				has_building = building_financial_centre_spa
				has_building = building_financial_centre_swe
				has_building = building_financial_centre_swi
				has_building = building_financial_centre_tus
				has_building = building_financial_centre_tur
				has_building = building_financial_centre_uru
				has_building = building_financial_centre_usa
				has_building = building_financial_centre_usa_2
				has_building = building_financial_centre_sax
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = has_financial_center
        add_modifier = {
            name = has_financial_center
			multiplier = value_for_has_financial_center
        }
    }

	financial_center_production_methods = yes
	#building - # supply demand for financial product
	random_scope_building = {
		limit = {
			is_building_group = bg_financial_centre
		}

		remove_modifier = bond_deemande
        add_modifier = {
            name = bond_deemande
			multiplier = target_demand_bond_for_modifier
        }
		remove_modifier = manufacture_stock_deemande
        add_modifier = {
            name = manufacture_stock_deemande
			multiplier = target_demand_manufacture_stock_for_modifier
        }
		remove_modifier = agricultural_stock_deemande
        add_modifier = {
            name = agricultural_stock_deemande
			multiplier = target_demand_agricultural_stock_for_modifier
        }
		remove_modifier = mining_stock_deemande
        add_modifier = {
            name = mining_stock_deemande
			multiplier = target_demand_mining_stock_for_modifier
        }
		remove_modifier = railroad_stock_deemande
        add_modifier = {
            name = railroad_stock_deemande
			multiplier = target_demand_railroad_stock_for_modifier
        }

		remove_modifier = mutual_fund_supply
        add_modifier = {
            name = mutual_fund_supply
			multiplier = target_supply_mutual_fund_for_modifier
        }

		if = {
			limit = {
				occupancy  < 0.75
				not = {
					owner = {
						is_player = yes
					}
				}
			}
			set_subsidized = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				occupancy > 0.75
				not = {
					owner = {
						is_player = yes
					}
				}
			}
			set_subsidized = no
		}
	}

	#####################################################################################################################################################
	# ban good
	######################
	#bond
	if = {
		limit = { #tech à ajouter ici permet de délock l'import de pf étrangé au dela de 25%
			market.mg:bond.market_goods_imports > bond_market_goods_sell_orders_ratio
		}
		add_banned_goods = g:bond
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			market.mg:bond.market_goods_imports < bond_market_goods_sell_orders_ratio
		}
		remove_banned_goods = g:bond
	}

	######################
	#manufacture_stock
	if = {
		limit = { #tech à ajouter ici permet de délock l'import de pf étrangé au dela de 25%
			market.mg:manufacture_stock.market_goods_imports > manufacture_stock_market_goods_sell_orders_ratio
		}
		add_banned_goods = g:manufacture_stock
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			market.mg:manufacture_stock.market_goods_imports < manufacture_stock_market_goods_sell_orders_ratio
		}
		remove_banned_goods = g:manufacture_stock
	}

	######################
	#manufacture_stock
	if = {
		limit = { #tech à ajouter ici permet de délock l'import de pf étrangé au dela de 25%
			market.mg:manufacture_stock.market_goods_imports > manufacture_stock_market_goods_sell_orders_ratio
		}
		add_banned_goods = g:manufacture_stock
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			market.mg:manufacture_stock.market_goods_imports < manufacture_stock_market_goods_sell_orders_ratio
		}
		remove_banned_goods = g:manufacture_stock
	}
	######################
	######################
	#agricultural_stock
	if = {
		limit = { #tech à ajouter ici permet de délock l'import de pf étrangé au dela de 25%
			market.mg:agricultural_stock.market_goods_imports > agricultural_stock_market_goods_sell_orders_ratio
		}
		add_banned_goods = g:agricultural_stock
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			market.mg:agricultural_stock.market_goods_imports < agricultural_stock_market_goods_sell_orders_ratio
		}
		remove_banned_goods = g:agricultural_stock
	}
	######################
	######################
	#mining_stock
	if = {
		limit = { #tech à ajouter ici permet de délock l'import de pf étrangé au dela de 25%
			market.mg:mining_stock.market_goods_imports > mining_stock_market_goods_sell_orders_ratio
		}
		add_banned_goods = g:mining_stock
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			market.mg:mining_stock.market_goods_imports < mining_stock_market_goods_sell_orders_ratio
		}
		remove_banned_goods = g:mining_stock
	}
	######################

	#railroad_stock
	if = {

			market.mg:railroad_stock.market_goods_imports > railroad_stock_market_goods_sell_orders_ratio
		}
		add_banned_goods = g:railroad_stock
	}
	if = {

		}
		remove_banned_goods = g:railroad_stock
	}
	######################

	if = { #country_already_financial_center
		limit = {
			or = {
				has_building = building_financial_centre
				has_building = building_financial_centre_arg
				has_building = building_financial_centre_aus
				has_building = building_financial_centre_bav
				has_building = building_financial_centre_bel
				has_building = building_financial_centre_bic
				has_building = building_financial_centre_brz
				has_building = building_financial_centre_chi
				has_building = building_financial_centre_chl
				has_building = building_financial_centre_den
				has_building = building_financial_centre_dei
				has_building = building_financial_centre_egy
				has_building = building_financial_centre_fra
				has_building = building_financial_centre_frm
				has_building = building_financial_centre_gbr
				has_building = building_financial_centre_gbr_2
				has_building = building_financial_centre_gre
				has_building = building_financial_centre_hkh
				has_building = building_financial_centre_han
				has_building = building_financial_centre_ita
				has_building = building_financial_centre_jap

national_stockpile_modifier = {
	capital = {
		save_scope_as = capital_scope
	}
	every_scope_state = { #historic_place jamais netoyer
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = national_stockpile_place
			}
			remove_modifier = national_stockpile_place
		}
	}
	scope:capital_scope = { #actualisation capital
		#place
		if = {
			limit = {
				not = {
					has_modifier = national_stockpile_place
				}
			}
			remove_modifier = national_stockpile_place
			add_modifier = {
				name = national_stockpile_place
			}
		}
		#historic_place
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = national_stockpile_place
			}
			remove_modifier = national_stockpile_historic_place
			add_modifier = {
				name = national_stockpile_historic_place
			}
		}
	}
	if = { #country - une seul fois
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}
			not  = {
				has_modifier = has_national_stockpile
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = has_national_stockpile
		}
	}
	if = { #country_already_national_stockpile
		limit = {
			has_building = building_national_stockpile
			not  = {
				var:country_already_national_stockpile = 1
			}
		}
		set_variable  = {
			name = country_already_national_stockpile
			value = 1
		}
	}
}
remove_country_building_modifier = { #country

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
			NOT = {
				any_scope_state = {
					has_building = building_bank
				}
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = has_central_bank
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = has_financial_center
			NOT = {
				any_scope_state = {
					or = {
						has_building = building_financial_centre
						has_building = building_financial_centre_arg
						has_building = building_financial_centre_aus
						has_building = building_financial_centre_bav
						has_building = building_financial_centre_bel
						has_building = building_financial_centre_bic
						has_building = building_financial_centre_brz
						has_building = building_financial_centre_chi
						has_building = building_financial_centre_chl
						has_building = building_financial_centre_den
						has_building = building_financial_centre_dei
						has_building = building_financial_centre_egy
						has_building = building_financial_centre_fra
						has_building = building_financial_centre_frm
						has_building = building_financial_centre_gbr
						has_building = building_financial_centre_gbr_2
						has_building = building_financial_centre_gre
						has_building = building_financial_centre_hkh
						has_building = building_financial_centre_han
						has_building = building_financial_centre_ita
						has_building = building_financial_centre_jap
						has_building = building_financial_centre_mex
						has_building = building_financial_centre_net
						has_building = building_financial_centre_nsw
						has_building = building_financial_centre_ont
						has_building = building_financial_centre_peu
						has_building = building_financial_centre_por
						has_building = building_financial_centre_pru
						has_building = building_financial_centre_que
						has_building = building_financial_centre_rus
						has_building = building_financial_centre_saf
						has_building = building_financial_centre_sar
						has_building = building_financial_centre_sic
						has_building = building_financial_centre_spa
						has_building = building_financial_centre_swe
						has_building = building_financial_centre_swi
						has_building = building_financial_centre_tus
						has_building = building_financial_centre_tur
						has_building = building_financial_centre_uru
						has_building = building_financial_centre_usa
						has_building = building_financial_centre_usa_2
						has_building = building_financial_centre_sax
					}
				}
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = has_financial_center
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = has_national_stockpile
			NOT = {
				any_scope_state = {
					has_building = building_national_stockpile
				}
			}
		}
		remove_modifier = has_national_stockpile
	}
}
reset_building = {
	root  = {
		remove_country_building_modifier = yes
		has_tech_central_bank_but_no_building_central_bank = yes
		has_tech_financial_center_but_no_building_financial_center = yes
		national_stockpile_1 = yes

		stockpiling_capital_state_transfert = yes
	}
}
destroy_building_not_allowed = {
	every_scope_state = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				and = {
					has_building = building_bank
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = central_bank_place
					}
				}
			}
			remove_building = building_bank
			reset_building = yes
		}
        if = {
            limit = {
                and = {
                    has_building = building_financial_centre
                    NOT = {
                        has_modifier = financial_center_place
                    }
                }
            }
            remove_building = building_financial_centre
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                and = {
                    has_building = building_national_stockpile
                    NOT = {
                        has_modifier = national_stockpile_place
                    }
                }
            }
            remove_building = building_national_stockpile
        }
	}
}

initialize_historic_macro_facilities_bc = { #history
	add_technology_researched = banking
	add_technology_researched = currency_standards
	add_technology_researched = central_banking
	add_technology_researched = metalique_standard

	$CTRL_BANK_SITE$ = {
		create_building = {
			building = $BANK_BLDG_TYPE$
			level    = $CB_SIZE$
			reserves = 1
		}
		owner = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = has_central_bank
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = central_bank_location
				value = $CTRL_BANK_SITE$
			}
		}
	} 
	central_bank_modifier = yes
}
initialize_historic_macro_facilities_fc = { #history
	add_technology_researched = financial_center
	add_technology_researched = stock_exchange

	$FIN_CENT_SITE$ = {
		create_building = {
			building = $FIN_BLDG_TYPE$
			level    = $FC_SIZE$
			reserves = 1
		}
		owner = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = has_financial_center
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = financial_center_location
				value = $FIN_CENT_SITE$
			}
		}
	}
	#update_modifiers_bc_fc_ns = yes
	financial_center_modifier = yes

}
initialize_historic_macro_facilities_ns = {  #history
	add_technology_researched = stockpiling_goods
	add_technology_researched = national_stockpile

	$STOCKPILE_SITE$ = {
		create_building = {
			building = building_national_stockpile
			level = 1
		}
		owner = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = has_national_stockpile
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = stockpile_location
				value = $STOCKPILE_SITE$
			}
		}
	}
	#update_modifiers_bc_fc_ns = yes
	national_stockpile_modifier = yes

}

macro_facilities_on_action_bc = {
	if = {
		limit = { ### check to make sure we're ready and stable enough
			macro_facilities_on_action_bc_limit = yes
		}
		macro_facilities_bc = {
			CTRL_BANK_SITE = capital
			BANK_BLDG_TYPE = building_bank
		}
	}
}
macro_facilities_bc = {
	#for country witch is_valid_country = yes but GDP < 5M
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_technology_researched = central_banking
			var:gdp_view < 1
		}
		$CTRL_BANK_SITE$ = {
			create_building = {
				building = $BANK_BLDG_TYPE$
				level    = 5
				reserves=1
			}
		}
	}

	#general
	switch = {
		trigger = var:gdp_view
		1 = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_technology_researched = central_banking }

has_tech_central_bank_but_no_building_central_bank = {
	### redundancy: treated in event central_bank_event.1
	capital = {
		save_scope_as = central_bank_site
	}
	if = {
		limit = { ### check to make sure we're ready and stable enough
			macro_facilities_on_action_bc_limit = yes
			not = { #vérifit si le modifier n'existe pas -> pas sure
				has_modifier = has_central_bank
			}
		}
		macro_facilities_on_action_bc = yes
	}
}
has_currency_law_but_no_building_central_bank = {
	### redundancy: treated in event central_bank_event.1
	capital = {

			has_technology_researched = central_banking
			is_revolutionary =  no

				is_valid_country = yes

#####################################################################################################################################################
#reparation after crisi
#####################################################################################################################################################
central_bank_respawn_after_crisis = {
	$CTRL_BANK_SITE$ = {
		create_building = {
			building = $BANK_BLDG_TYPE$
			level    = $CB_SIZE$
			reserves = 1
		}
	}
}

macro_facilities_on_action_fc = { #comme il n'y a plus de niveau macro_facilities_on_action_fc n'est plus dans le on_action

		limit = { ### check to make sure we're ready and stable enough

		}
		#arg
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BUENOS_AIRES

has_second_financial_center = { #est utilisé pourr fairre apparaitre les centrre financier si il n'existe plus
	if = {
		limit = {
			#macro_facilities_on_action_fc_limit = yes
			has_technology_researched = financial_center
			has_modifier = has_financial_center
			is_invalid_country = no
			is_revolutionary =  no
			or = { #???????????????????????????????????????????????
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BUENOS_AIRES
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_AUSTRIA
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BAVARIA
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_FLANDERS
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BOMBAY
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_RIO_DE_JANEIRO
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_SUZHOU
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_SANTIAGO
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ZEALAND
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_WEST_JAVA
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_LOWER_EGYPT
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ILE_DE_FRANCE
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_HESSE
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_HOME_COUNTIES
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_LANCASHIRE
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ATTICA
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_SHAOZHOU
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_HANNOVER
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_LOMBARDY
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_KANTO
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MEXICO
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_HOLLAND
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_NEW_SOUTH_WALES
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ONTARIO
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_LIMA
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ESTREMADURA
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BRANDENBURG
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_QUEBEC
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_INGRIA
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_CAPE_COLONY
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_PIEDMONT
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_CAMPANIA
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_TOLEDO
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_SVEALAND
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_WEST_SWITZERLAND
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_EASTERN_THRACE
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_TUSCANY
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_URUGUAY
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_NEW_YORK
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ILLINOIS
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_SAXONY
			}
		}
		macro_facilities_on_action_fc = yes
	}
}
macro_facilities_fc = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_technology_researched = financial_center }
		$FIN_CENT_SITE$ = {
			create_building = {
				building = $FIN_BLDG_TYPE$
				level    = 5
				reserves=1
			}
		}
		financial_center_modifier = yes
	}
}

#brace
	macro_facilities_fc_arg = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_technology_researched = financial_center
				#has_financial_center = no
			}
			every_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					this = { state_region = s:STATE_BUENOS_AIRES }
				}
				create_building = {
					building = building_financial_centre_arg
					level    = 5
					reserves=1
				}
			}
			financial_center_modifier = yes
		}
	}

#####################################################################################################################################################
has_tech_financial_center_but_no_building_financial_center = { #est utilisé pourr fairre apparaitre les centrre financier si il n'existe plus
	if = {
		limit = {
			macro_facilities_on_action_fc_limit = yes
			not = { #vérifit si le modifier n'existe pas -> pas sure
				has_modifier = has_financial_center
			}
		}
		macro_facilities_on_action_fc = yes
	}

	# capital = {
	# 	save_scope_as = financial_center_site
	# }
}

#####################################################################################################################################################
#reparation after crisi
#####################################################################################################################################################
financial_center_respawn_after_crisis = {
	$FIN_CENT_SITE$ = {
		create_building = {
			building = $FIN_BLDG_TYPE$
			level    = $FC_SIZE$
			reserves = 1
		}
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################
#on_action
#####################################################################################################################################################
macro_facilities_on_action_ns = {
	if = {
		limit = { ### check to make sure we're ready and stable enough
			macro_facilities_on_action_ns_limit = yes
		}
		macro_facilities_ns = {
			NATIO_STOCK_SITE = capital
			NATIO_BLDG_TYPE = building_national_stockpile
		}
	}
}
macro_facilities_ns = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_technology_researched = national_stockpile }
		$NATIO_STOCK_SITE$ = {
			create_building = {
				building = $NATIO_BLDG_TYPE$
				level    = 1
				reserves=1
			}
		}
	}
	national_stockpile_modifier = yes
}

#financial_crash
financial_crash_destroy_financial_center = {
	every_scope_state = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_financial_centre
			}
			remove_building = building_financial_centre
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_financial_centre_arg
			}
			remove_building = building_financial_centre_arg
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_financial_centre_aus
			}
			remove_building = building_financial_centre_aus
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_financial_centre_bav
			}
			remove_building = building_financial_centre_bav
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_financial_centre_bel
			}
			remove_building = building_financial_centre_bel
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_financial_centre_bic
			}
			remove_building = building_financial_centre_bic
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_financial_centre_brz
			}
			remove_building = building_financial_centre_brz
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_financial_centre_chi
			}
			remove_building = building_financial_centre_chi
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_financial_centre_chl
			}
			remove_building = building_financial_centre_chl
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

#economic_crisis
economic_crisis_destroy_central_bank = {
	every_scope_state = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_bank
			}
			remove_building = building_bank
		}
	}
	central_bank_respawn_after_crisis = {
		CTRL_BANK_SITE = capital
		BANK_BLDG_TYPE = building_bank
		CB_SIZE        = 5
	}
}

#introduction_new_currency

###########################################################################################################################################################################################
###########################################################################################################################################################################################
###########################################################################################################################################################################################
###########################################################################################################################################################################################

introduction_new_currency = {
	if = { 
		limit = {
			not = {
				any_scope_state = {
					has_building = building_bank
				}
			}
		}  
		# gdp_view_on_action = yes
		# macro_facilities_on_action_bc = yes #pas le choix que de le codé en dure car trop d'interaction
		capital = {
			save_scope_as = central_bank_site
		}
		scope:central_bank_site = {
			create_building = {
				building = building_bank
				level = 5
				reserves=1
			}
		}
		central_bank_modifier = yes
		central_bank_production_methods = yes  
	}
 
	#Event for spe currency -> ef_introduction_events
	introduction_of_dinar = yes
	introduction_of_dinar_algerian_dinar = yes
	introduction_of_dinar_iraqi_dinar = yes
	introduction_of_dinar_libyan_dinar = yes
	introduction_of_dinar_moroccan_dirham = yes
	introduction_of_dinar_omanian_rial = yes
	introduction_of_dinar_qiran = yes
	introduction_of_dinar_saudi_riyal = yes
	introduction_of_dinar_serbian_dinar = yes
	introduction_of_dinar_tunisian_dinar = yes
	introduction_of_dinar_yugoslav_dinar = yes

		}
		money_value_global_var = yes
	}
}

#dinar
introduction_of_dinar = {
	if = {
		limit = { #Introduction of dinar
			currency_identifiers_dinar = 1
		}
		if = { #Current circulation of dinar
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_no_market_liquidity
			}
			capital = {
				save_scope_as = central_bank_site
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = money_value_target_1
				value = { 1 12 }
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = circulating_dinar_c_var_1
				add = { 50000009 100000009 }
			}
			scope:central_bank_site = {
				change_variable = {
					name = stockpiling_dinar_state_1
					add  = {
						value = owner.var:circulating_dinar_c_var_1
						multiply = 0.101
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = silver_state_1
					add = {
						value = owner.var:circulating_dinar_c_var_1
						add = var:stockpiling_dinar_state_1
						multiply = owner.var:money_value_target_1
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = gold_state_1
					add = {
						value = var:silver_state_1
						multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
					}
				}
			}
			activate_law = law_type:law_dinar_currency
		}
	}
}

				change_variable = {
					name = gold_state_1

			}

				add = { 50000009 100000009 }
			}
			scope:central_bank_site = {
				change_variable = {
					name = stockpiling_krone_czech_koruna_state_1
					add  = {
						value = owner.var:circulating_krone_czech_koruna_c_var_1

				save_scope_as = central_bank_site
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = money_value_target_1
				value = { 1 12 }
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = circulating_mark_c_var_1
				add = { 50000009 100000009 }
			}
			scope:central_bank_site = {
				change_variable = {
					name = stockpiling_mark_state_1
					add  = {
						value = owner.var:circulating_mark_c_var_1
						multiply = 0.101
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = silver_state_1
					add = {
						value = owner.var:circulating_mark_c_var_1
						add = var:stockpiling_mark_state_1
						multiply = owner.var:money_value_target_1
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = gold_state_1
					add = {
						value = var:silver_state_1
						multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
					}
				}
			}
			activate_law = law_type:law_mark_currency
		}
	}
}

#peso_paraguayan_peso
introduction_of_peso_paraguayan_peso = {
	if = {
		limit = { #Introduction of peso_paraguayan_peso
			currency_identifiers_peso_paraguayan_peso = 1
		}
		if = { #Current circulation of peso_paraguayan_peso
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_no_market_liquidity
			}
			capital = {
				save_scope_as = central_bank_site
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = money_value_target_1
				value = { 1 12 }
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = circulating_peso_paraguayan_peso_c_var_1
				add = { 50000009 100000009 }
			}
			scope:central_bank_site = {
				change_variable = {
					name = stockpiling_peso_paraguayan_peso_state_1
					add  = {
						value = owner.var:circulating_peso_paraguayan_peso_c_var_1
						multiply = 0.101
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = silver_state_1
					add = {
						value = owner.var:circulating_peso_paraguayan_peso_c_var_1
						add = var:stockpiling_peso_paraguayan_peso_state_1
						multiply = owner.var:money_value_target_1
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = gold_state_1
					add = {
						value = var:silver_state_1
						multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
					}
				}
			}
			activate_law = law_type:law_peso_paraguayan_peso_currency
		}
	}
}

				has_law = law_type:law_no_market_liquidity
			}
			capital = {
				save_scope_as = central_bank_site
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = money_value_target_1
				value = { 1 12 }
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = circulating_spe_korean_won_c_var_1
				add = { 50000009 100000009 }
			}
			scope:central_bank_site = {
				change_variable = {
					name = stockpiling_spe_korean_won_state_1
					add  = {
						value = owner.var:circulating_spe_korean_won_c_var_1
						multiply = 0.101
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = silver_state_1
					add = {
						value = owner.var:circulating_spe_korean_won_c_var_1
						add = var:stockpiling_spe_korean_won_state_1
						multiply = owner.var:money_value_target_1
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = gold_state_1
					add = {
						value = var:silver_state_1
						multiply = silver_to_gold_rate
					}
				}
			}
			activate_law = law_type:law_spe_korean_won_currency
		}
	}
}
